style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, Laclede reported an increase in consolidated net income to </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$84.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$2.35</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$2.02</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share) for fiscal 2013. Net economic earnings (&#8220;NEE&#8221;) for 2014 were </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$100.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$3.05</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share), up from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$65.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$2.87</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share) for the prior year, an increase of 6.3 percent on a per share basis. NEE excludes from net income the effect of unrealized gains and losses on energy-related derivatives, as well as the impacts of the Missouri Gas Energy (&#8220;MGE&#8221;) and Alagasco acquisitions. Those impacts include acquisition-related costs, the results of operations for the month of September for Alagasco in 2014 and MGE in 2013, interest expense in the year of acquisition on long-term debt issued to finance the transactions, and the dilutive impact in the year of issuance of the approximately 10 million shares issued in both 2014 and 2013 in conjunction with the acquisitions. The increase in NEE from 2013 to 2014 was driven primarily by improved Gas Utility performance, reflecting the addition of MGE, and higher earnings in the Gas Marketing segment driven by colder weather.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Gas Utility</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Gas Utility segment includes the regulated gas distribution operations of our legacy Laclede Gas business and MGE, and for the month of September 2014, Alagasco. For the fiscal year ended September 30, 2014, the Gas Utility segment reported NEE of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$92.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, up from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$56.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior fiscal year. Segment net income was </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$87.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, up from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$56.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in  2013. The improvement was driven by a </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$222.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increase in operating  margin (non-GAAP; see &#8220;Operating Margin and Reconciliation to GAAP&#8221; on page 11), of which $186.5 million is attributable to the addition of MGE, and $14.8 million is due to the acquisition of Alagasco. The remaining increase is largely due to increased margins from off-system and propane sales reflecting colder weather, as well as increases in Infrastructure System Replacement Surcharge (ISRS) and base rates. Other operating expenses increased by </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$124.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, of which $103.5 million is due to MGE and $14.2 million is due to Alagasco. The increase in expenses reflects the impacts of colder weather such as higher costs for bad debt, maintenance and labor. Depreciation and amortization expense increased by </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$34.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, with $29.9 million attributable to MGE and Alagasco, and the remainder reflecting capital investments.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Gas Marketing</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Gas Marketing segment includes the results of Laclede Energy Resources, which provides natural gas marketing services to the Midwest region. Full year fiscal 2014 NEE increased to </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$10.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$8.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year, while net income increased to </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$12.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$7.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">. The increase in earnings was largely due to higher weather-related operating margins in the fiscal second quarter reflecting extreme cold temperatures, partially offset by the expiration of two favorable gas supply contracts during fiscal 2013 and early fiscal 2014.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><div style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#32;2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s22FC7A623A5D803F02A2E7991FCEAE4D"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;padding-top:6px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">For the fourth quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, Laclede reported a consolidated net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$14.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.35</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;&#32;per share), compared to a net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$9.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.30</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share) for the same period last year. Net losses for the quarters reflect acquisition-related impacts, including after-tax costs of $11.2 million in 2014 and $5.5 million in 2013 that are excluded to derive NEE. Fourth quarter NEE improved to a loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$2.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.07</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share) from a loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$3.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.17</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share) a year ago. The Gas Utility segment</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s earnings are seasonal in nature and generally correspond to the heating season. As a result, the segment typically reports a loss in the fiscal fourth quarter. The increase in NEE was driven by a smaller seasonal loss from Gas Utility reflecting the inclusion in 2014 of MGE</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s results which are less impacted by seasonality than those of Laclede Gas. The better Gas Utility earnings were partially offset by lower operating results from Gas Marketing, and a loss in the Other segment compared to essentially breakeven in the prior-year quarter. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Gas Utility</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Gas Utility segment posted a net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$4.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2014, compared to a net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$6.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the same period last year. On an NEE basis, the segment reported a quarterly loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$1.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in 2014, compared to a larger loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$5.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in 2013. The improvement in NEE was primarily due to a </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$46.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increase in operating margin, of which $30.3 million and $14.8 million were attributable to the addition of MGE and Alagasco, respectively. The improvement also reflects $1.7 million related to higher ISRS revenues, partially offset by a modest decline in consumption. Other operating expenses and deductions increased by $28.6 million, with $20.1 million and $14.2 million due to the inclusion of MGE and Alagasco, respectively.   Depreciation and amortization increased </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$9.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, with $4.8 million due to MGE and $3.9 million related to Alagasco.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Gas Marketing</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Fourth quarter NEE was </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, down from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$1.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year period, while Gas Marketing reported a net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$0.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to net income of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$1.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the fourth quarter of 2013. Results for Gas Marketing are largely driven by opportunities created by price volatility and basis differentials (pricing differences between supply regions). Operating margin for the fourth quarter declined by </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$3.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;reflecting lower sales margins, due to market conditions and the expiration of a favorable gas supply contract, partially offset by slightly higher volumes.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">ACQUISITION-RELATED COSTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The after-tax impact of acquisition-related costs (primarily for the evaluation and negotiation of transactions and net one-time integration costs) is excluded from GAAP results for NEE purposes. See reconciliation on page 10. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Missouri Gas Energy</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Since closing the acquisition in late fiscal 2013, the Company has incurred costs for the integration of MGE. Those costs totaled $5.6 million for the full year 2014 and $1.0 million in the fiscal fourth quarter. Under the regulatory order approving the MGE acquisition, Laclede Gas defers for future rate recovery 50 percent of these costs, resulting in a deferral of $2.8 million for the full year and $0.5 million  for the fourth quarter. The after-tax impacts of the net one-time integration costs were $1.7 million and $0.3 million, respectively. For fiscal 2013, MGE integration costs occurred in the fourth quarter only and totaled $3.4 million ($1.7 million after deferral and $1.0 million after tax).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">For fiscal 2013, total acquisition-related costs were $17.4 million ($10.8 million after tax, or $0.42 per share) for the full year and $8.9 million ($5.5 million after tax, or $0.17 per share) in the fourth quarter. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Alagasco</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Laclede closed on the acquisition of Alagasco on September 2, 2014, with an effective date of August 31, 2014. In fiscal 2014, the Company incurred transaction costs for Alagasco totaling $15.5 million ($9.9 million after tax) for the full year and $9.8 million ($6.2 million after tax) in the fourth quarter. The Company incurred total transaction-related costs of $19.0 million, including interest costs associated with the long-term debt issued to finance the acquisition.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#32;3</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s22FC7A623A5D803F02A2E7991FCEAE4D"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">REGULATORY UPDATE</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Effective October 18, 2014, the Missouri Public Service Commission (MoPSC) approved an ISRS increase for Laclede Gas of $2.8 million annually, covering additional investments in its distribution system since the ISRS was established effective April 12, 2014. As a result, authorized annual recoveries under the ISRS for Laclede Gas now stand at $9.8 million.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Also effective October 18, 2014, the MoPSC approved the establishment of a new ISRS of $2.0 million annually for MGE.  The ISRS for MGE had been reset to zero with the settlement of its rate case effective May 1, 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">BALANCE SHEETS AND CASH FLOWS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The balance sheet for Laclede as of </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;&#32;reflects the acquisition of Alagasco</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s assets effective August 31, 2014, including the allocation of the $1.60 billion purchase price to tangible and intangible assets and the assumption of certain liabilities. Laclede maintains a strong capital structure with ample liquidity and access to short term borrowing to meet its anticipated ongoing capital needs. The change in the Company</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s capitalization reflects the combined effect of the Company</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s issuance of both equity and debt in each of the last two fiscal years to fund the acquisitions of MGE and Alagasco. Short-term borrowings outstanding at </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;under new or recently-extended credit facilities were </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$287.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$74.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;at the end of fiscal 2013. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The net cash provided by operating activities was </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$122.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in 2014, down from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$163.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year. The decrease is primarily due to the inclusion of MGE gas cost under the Purchased Gas Adjustment Clause for a full year in 2014, the cash paid on interest rate swaps and the change in accounts payable as well as other working capital. These increases were partially offset by the increase in net income reflecting the addition of MGE and colder weather, and higher depreciation and amortization also reflecting the inclusion of MGE.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">Capital expenditures for 2014 increased to </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$171.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, including $7.7 million for Alagasco, from </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">$130.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior year. The increase was driven by a higher level of planned investment in ongoing accelerated distribution pipeline replacement at Laclede Gas and MGE, which totaled 139 miles up from 68 miles in 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">For additional details on Laclede</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s results for the fourth quarter and full year of fiscal 2014, please see the accompanying unaudited Statements of Consolidated Income, unaudited Condensed Consolidated Balance Sheets, and unaudited Condensed Statements of Consolidated Cash Flows.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">OUTLOOK</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Company reaffirms its long-term NEE per share growth target of between 4 percent and 6 percent first introduced earlier in 2014.  It also anticipates that growth in fiscal 2015 and 2016 will be above that target range after excluding the 2014 weather benefit of $0.17 per share recognized by the Gas Marketing segment.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">With the addition of Alagasco, the earnings mix and seasonality is anticipated to change in 2015.  Combined with the higher share count and the anticipated accretion from Alagasco, the Gas Utility segment is anticipated to grow from approximately 93 percent of total NEE per share to approximately 98 percent.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Company</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s earnings are also anticipated to become more concentrated in the heating season, reflecting Alagasco</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s rate design.  The percentage of full-year NEE per share earned in each quarter for fiscal 2014 actual (excluding weather benefit) and fiscal 2015 anticipated, are as follows:</font></div><div The Conference ID is 33716590. The webcast will be available for replay beginning November 26, at </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">www.TheLacledeGroup.com</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">ABOUT THE LACLEDE GROUP</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">The Laclede Group, Inc. (NYSE: LG), headquartered in St. Louis, Missouri, is a public utility holding company whose primary business is the safe and reliable delivery of natural gas service to more than 1.56 million residential, commercial and industrial customers across Missouri and Alabama. Its Gas Utility segment consists of three natural gas utilities: Laclede Gas Company (serving St. Louis and eastern Missouri), Missouri Gas Energy (serving Kansas City and western Missouri) and Alabama Gas Corporation (serving 186 cities and Alabama communities including Birmingham and Montgomery). Laclede</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">s non-utility businesses include Laclede Energy Resources, Inc., providing non-regulated natural gas services, and Spire which provides compressed natural gas (CNG) fueling solutions for transportation fleets. Laclede Group is committed to pursuing growth through 1) investing in infrastructure; 2) organically growing its existing businesses; 3) acquiring businesses to which the Company can apply its operating model and natural gas industry expertise, and 4) developing and investing in CNG fueling and other technologies. For more information about Laclede and its subsidiaries, visit&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">www.TheLacledeGroup.com</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">CAUTIONARY STATEMENTS ON FORWARD-LOOKING INFORMATION AND NON-GAAP MEASURES</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">This news release contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended. The Company's future operating results may be affected by various uncertainties and risk factors, many of which are beyond the Company's control, including weather conditions, economic factors, the competitive environment, governmental and regulatory policy and action, and risks associated with the acquisition and integration of MGE and Alagasco. For a more complete description of these uncertainties and risk factors, see the Company's Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended </font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">, filed later today with the Securities and Exchange Commission. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">This news release includes the non-GAAP financial measures of &#8220;net economic earnings,&#8221; and &#8220;net economic earnings per share,&#8221; and &#8220;operating margins.&#8221; Management also uses these non-GAAP measures internally when evaluating the Company's performance and results of operations. Net economic earnings exclude from net income the after-tax impacts of fair value accounting and timing adjustments associated with energy-related transactions. These adjustments, which primarily impact the Gas Marketing segment, include net unrealized gains and losses on energy-related derivatives resulting from the current changes in the fair value of financial and physical transactions prior to their completion and settlement, lower of cost or market inventory adjustments, and realized gains and losses on economic hedges prior to the sale of the physical commodity. In calculating net economic earnings, </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#32;5</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s22FC7A623A5D803F02A2E7991FCEAE4D"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">management also excludes from net income the after-tax impacts related to acquisition, divestiture, and restructuring activities, including one-time costs related to the integration of MGE and costs related to the acquisition of Alagasco. Net economic earnings also exclude operating results for September, the last month of the fiscal year and the month in which the acquisitions were effective, for MGE in 2013 and Alagasco in 2014. Management believes that excluding these items provides a useful representation of the economic impact of actual settled transactions and overall results of ongoing operations. In calculating net economic earnings per share, management excludes from the weighted average number of shares the impact in each respective fiscal year of the equity issuances completed in May 2013 and June 2014 to support the financing of the acquisition of MGE and Alagasco, respectively. Management believes that these presentations provide a useful representation of operating performance by facilitating comparisons of year-over-year results. Operating margin adjusts operating income to include only those costs that are directly passed on to customers and collected through revenues, which are the wholesale cost of natural gas and propane and gross receipts taxes. These internal non-GAAP operating metrics should not be considered as an alternative to, or more meaningful than, GAAP measures such as operating income or net income.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font
